```markdown
- The best setting candidates are usually found by reducing slow-to-profit entries, not simply maximizing raw entry count.
- Focus first on buckets with low average PnL or long median hold time, then test stricter RSI/ADX/VWAP/VIX filters against those buckets.

```

Return JSON only. Think like a quant strategist:
- Identify which edges are real enough to protect.
- Identify which profiles are tail-heavy, dead, duplicated, or under-tested.
- Propose several next experiments, but keep them as research directions, not concrete config keys.
- Put requires-code/new-profile ideas in new_strategy_ideas, not in config changes.
- You may mention dormant profiles from the activation context as config-only activation candidates.
- Do not mention any other profiles absent from the active router lists unless explicitly saying they are inactive and should not be optimized.
